scripted_gui = {
   modifiergui_generated_scriptedgui_menu = {

        context_type = player_context
        window_name = "modifiergui_generated_window_menu"

        visible = {
            has_country_flag = modifiergui_core_guiflag_menu
        }

        effects = {

            closebutton_click = {
                modifiergui_windowcollapse_menu = yes
            }
            escapebutton_click = {
                if = {
                    limit = {
                        check_variable = { modifiergui_generated_guivar_menu = 0 }
                    }
                        modifiergui_windowcollapse_menu = yes
                }
            }
			categorybutton_politics_click = {
                if = {
                    limit = {
                        check_variable = { modifiergui_generated_guivar_menu = 1 }
                    }
                        modifiergui_windowcollapse_category_politics = yes
                }
                else = {
                    modifiergui_windowcollapse_menu_categories = yes
                    set_variable = { modifiergui_generated_guivar_menu = 1 }
                }
                modifiergui_generated_buttongloweffect_menu = yes
            }
			categorybutton_diplomacy_click = {
                if = {
                    limit = {
                        check_variable = { modifiergui_generated_guivar_menu = 2 }
                    }
                        modifiergui_windowcollapse_category_diplomacy = yes
                }
                else = {
                    modifiergui_windowcollapse_menu_categories = yes
                    set_variable = { modifiergui_generated_guivar_menu = 2 }
                }
                modifiergui_generated_buttongloweffect_menu = yes
            }
			categorybutton_industry_click = {
                if = {
                    limit = {
                        check_variable = { modifiergui_generated_guivar_menu = 3 }
                    }
                        modifiergui_windowcollapse_category_industry = yes
                }
                else = {

    modifiergui_generated_scriptedgui_category_politics = {

	modifiergui_generated_scriptedgui_modifier_political_power_factor = {

        context_type = player_context
        window_name = "modifiergui_generated_window_modifier_political_power_factor"

        visible = {
            check_variable = { modifiergui_generated_guivar_category_politics = 1 }
        }

        effects = {

            closebutton_click = {
                set_variable = { modifiergui_generated_guivar_category_politics = 0 }
                modifiergui_generated_buttongloweffect_category_politics = yes
            }
            escapebutton_click = {
                set_variable = { modifiergui_generated_guivar_category_politics = 0 }
                modifiergui_generated_buttongloweffect_category_politics = yes
            }

            button_counter_shift_click = {

                set_variable = { modifiergui_generated_modifiervar_political_power_factor = 0 }

            }

            button_downvar_click = {
                modifiergui_generated_applydynamicmodifier_political_power_factor = yes
                subtract_from_variable = { modifiergui_generated_modifiervar_political_power_factor = 0.01 }
            }
            button_downvar_control_click = {
                modifiergui_generated_applydynamicmodifier_political_power_factor = yes
                subtract_from_variable = { modifiergui_generated_modifiervar_political_power_factor = 0.1 }
            }
            button_downvar_shift_click = {
                modifiergui_generated_applydynamicmodifier_political_power_factor = yes
                subtract_from_variable = { modifiergui_generated_modifiervar_political_power_factor = 1 }
            }
            button_downvar_control_shift_click = {
                modifiergui_generated_applydynamicmodifier_political_power_factor = yes
                subtract_from_variable = { modifiergui_generated_modifiervar_political_power_factor = 10 }
            }

            button_upvar_click = {
                modifiergui_generated_applydynamicmodifier_political_power_factor = yes
                add_to_variable = { modifiergui_generated_modifiervar_political_power_factor = 0.01 }
            }
            button_upvar_control_click = {
                modifiergui_generated_applydynamicmodifier_political_power_factor = yes
                add_to_variable = { modifiergui_generated_modifiervar_political_power_factor = 0.1 }
            }
            button_upvar_shift_click = {
                modifiergui_generated_applydynamicmodifier_political_power_factor = yes
                add_to_variable = { modifiergui_generated_modifiervar_political_power_factor = 1 }
            }
            button_upvar_control_shift_click = {
                modifiergui_generated_applydynamicmodifier_political_power_factor = yes
                add_to_variable = { modifiergui_generated_modifiervar_political_power_factor = 10 }
            }


        }

    }

    modifiergui_generated_scriptedgui_category_production = {

        context_type = player_context
        window_name = "modifiergui_generated_window_category_production"

        visible = {
            check_variable = { modifiergui_generated_guivar_menu = 4 }
        }

        effects = {
            closebutton_click = {
                modifiergui_windowcollapse_category_production = yes
                modifiergui_generated_buttongloweffect_menu = yes
            }
            escapebutton_click = {
                if = {
                    limit = {
                        check_variable = { modifiergui_generated_guivar_category_production = 0 }
                    }
                        modifiergui_windowcollapse_category_production = yes
                        modifiergui_generated_buttongloweffect_category_production = yes
                        modifiergui_generated_buttongloweffect_menu = yes
                }
            }
			modifierbutton_production_factory_max_efficiency_factor_click = {
                if = {
                    limit = {
                        check_variable = { modifiergui_generated_guivar_category_production = 1 }
                    }
                    set_variable = { modifiergui_generated_guivar_category_production = 0 }
                }
                else = {
                    set_variable = { modifiergui_generated_guivar_category_production = 1 }
                }
                modifiergui_generated_buttongloweffect_category_production = yes
            }
			modifierbutton_production_factory_efficiency_gain_factor_click = {
                if = {
                    limit = {
                        check_variable = { modifiergui_generated_guivar_category_production = 2 }
                    }
                    set_variable = { modifiergui_generated_guivar_category_production = 0 }
                }
                else = {
                    set_variable = { modifiergui_generated_guivar_category_production = 2 }
                }
                modifiergui_generated_buttongloweffect_category_production = yes

        }

        effects = {

                set_variable = { modifiergui_generated_guivar_category_army = 0 }
                modifiergui_generated_buttongloweffect_category_army = yes

                modifiergui_generated_buttongloweffect_category_army = yes
            }

            }

            button_downvar_click = {
                modifiergui_generated_applydynamicmodifier_army_attack_factor = yes
                subtract_from_variable = { modifiergui_generated_modifiervar_army_attack_factor = 0.01 }
            }
            button_downvar_control_click = {
                modifiergui_generated_applydynamicmodifier_army_attack_factor = yes
                subtract_from_variable = { modifiergui_generated_modifiervar_army_attack_factor = 0.1 }
            }
            button_downvar_shift_click = {
                modifiergui_generated_applydynamicmodifier_army_attack_factor = yes
                subtract_from_variable = { modifiergui_generated_modifiervar_army_attack_factor = 1 }
            }
            button_downvar_control_shift_click = {
                modifiergui_generated_applydynamicmodifier_army_attack_factor = yes
                subtract_from_variable = { modifiergui_generated_modifiervar_army_attack_factor = 10 }
            }

            button_upvar_click = {
                modifiergui_generated_applydynamicmodifier_army_attack_factor = yes
                add_to_variable = { modifiergui_generated_modifiervar_army_attack_factor = 0.01 }
            }
            button_upvar_control_click = {
                modifiergui_generated_applydynamicmodifier_army_attack_factor = yes
                add_to_variable = { modifiergui_generated_modifiervar_army_attack_factor = 0.1 }

                modifiergui_generated_applydynamicmodifier_air_range_factor = yes

            button_downvar_shift_click = {
                modifiergui_generated_applydynamicmodifier_air_range_factor = yes
                subtract_from_variable = { modifiergui_generated_modifiervar_air_range_factor = 1 }
            }

                modifiergui_generated_applydynamicmodifier_air_range_factor = yes
                subtract_from_variable = { modifiergui_generated_modifiervar_air_range_factor = 10 }
            }

            button_upvar_click = {

    modifiergui_generated_scriptedgui_category_research = {

        context_type = player_context
        window_name = "modifiergui_generated_window_category_research"

        visible = {
            check_variable = { modifiergui_generated_guivar_menu = 10 }
        }

        effects = {
            closebutton_click = {
                modifiergui_windowcollapse_category_research = yes
                modifiergui_generated_buttongloweffect_menu = yes

                if = {
                    limit = {

	modifiergui_generated_scriptedgui_modifier_decryption_factor = {

        context_type = player_context
        window_name = "modifiergui_generated_window_modifier_decryption_factor"

        visible = {
            check_variable = { modifiergui_generated_guivar_category_espionage = 1 }
        }

        effects = {

            closebutton_click = {
                set_variable = { modifiergui_generated_guivar_category_espionage = 0 }
                modifiergui_generated_buttongloweffect_category_espionage = yes
            }
            escapebutton_click = {
                set_variable = { modifiergui_generated_guivar_category_espionage = 0 }
                modifiergui_generated_buttongloweffect_category_espionage = yes
            }

            button_counter_shift_click = {

                set_variable = { modifiergui_generated_modifiervar_decryption_factor = 0 }

            }

            button_downvar_click = {
                modifiergui_generated_applydynamicmodifier_decryption_factor = yes
                subtract_from_variable = { modifiergui_generated_modifiervar_decryption_factor = 0.01 }
            }
            button_downvar_control_click = {
                modifiergui_generated_applydynamicmodifier_decryption_factor = yes
                subtract_from_variable = { modifiergui_generated_modifiervar_decryption_factor = 0.1 }
            }
            button_downvar_shift_click = {
                modifiergui_generated_applydynamicmodifier_decryption_factor = yes
                subtract_from_variable = { modifiergui_generated_modifiervar_decryption_factor = 1 }
            }
            button_downvar_control_shift_click = {
                modifiergui_generated_applydynamicmodifier_decryption_factor = yes
                subtract_from_variable = { modifiergui_generated_modifiervar_decryption_factor = 10 }
            }

            button_upvar_click = {
                modifiergui_generated_applydynamicmodifier_decryption_factor = yes
                add_to_variable = { modifiergui_generated_modifiervar_decryption_factor = 0.01 }
            }
            button_upvar_control_click = {
                modifiergui_generated_applydynamicmodifier_decryption_factor = yes
                add_to_variable = { modifiergui_generated_modifiervar_decryption_factor = 0.1 }
            }
            button_upvar_shift_click = {
                modifiergui_generated_applydynamicmodifier_decryption_factor = yes
                add_to_variable = { modifiergui_generated_modifiervar_decryption_factor = 1 }
            }
            button_upvar_control_shift_click = {
                modifiergui_generated_applydynamicmodifier_decryption_factor = yes
                add_to_variable = { modifiergui_generated_modifiervar_decryption_factor = 10 }
            }


        }
